                    appId: "154672961283231",
                    status: true,
                    cookie: true,
                    oauth: true,
                    xfbml: true
                });
                FB.Event.subscribe('edge.create', function(href, widget){
                    // Do something, e.g. track the click on the "Like" button here
                    if (typeof(gameReportingInfo) != "undefined") {
                        GW.reporting.reportFBLike({
                            href: window.location.href,
                            state: "on"
                        }, gameReportingInfo);
                    }
                    else {
                        GW.reporting.reportFBLike({
                            href: window.location.href,
                            state: "on"
                        }, null);
                    }
                });
            };

    <script type="text/javascript">
    	$(function(){
    		var titles = $(".game-icon-80x60 .game-title");
    		for(var i = 0; i < titles.length;i++) {
    			var thisTitle = titles[i];
    			var containerHeight = $(thisTitle).height();
    			var titleHeight = $(thisTitle).children("div").height();
    			if(titleHeight > containerHeight) {
    				$(thisTitle).append("<div class='game-title-ellipsis'>...</div>");
    			}
    		}
    	});
    </script>
